    30	        private readonly Dictionary<StringSpanOrdinalKey, (int Id, string Token)> _vocab;
    31	        private IReadOnlyDictionary<string, int>? _vocabOriginal;
    32	        private const int MaxWordLengthToCache = 15;
    33	        private readonly PreTokenizer? _preTokenizer;
    34	        private readonly Normalizer? _normalizer;

    47	            this(string.IsNullOrEmpty(vocabFilePath) ? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(vocabFilePath)) : File.OpenRead(vocabFilePath), preTokenizer, specialTokens, normalizer, cacheSize, disposeStream: true)

    61	        internal TiktokenTokenizer(Stream vocabStream, PreTokenizer? preTokenizer, IReadOnlyDictionary<string, int>? specialTokens = null, Normalizer? normalizer = null, int cacheSize = LruCache<int[]>.DefaultCacheSize) :

    66	        /// <summary>
    67	        /// Create a new Tiktoken tokenizer's object.
    68	        /// </summary>
    69	        /// <param name="encoder">The dictionary mapping token utf-8 bytes to Ids.</param>
    70	        /// <param name="decoder">The dictionary mapping Ids to token utf-8 bytes.</param>
    71	        /// <param name="vocab">The dictionary mapping string tokens to Ids.</param>
    72	        /// <param name="preTokenizer">The pre-tokenizer to use.</param>
    73	        /// <param name="specialTokens">The dictionary mapping special tokens to Ids.</param>
    74	        /// <param name="normalizer">The normalizer to use.</param>
    75	        /// <param name="cacheSize">The max size of the cache to use.</param>
    76	        internal TiktokenTokenizer(
    77	            Dictionary<ReadOnlyMemory<byte>, int> encoder,
    78	            Dictionary<int, ReadOnlyMemory<byte>> decoder,
    79	            Dictionary<StringSpanOrdinalKey, (int Id, string Token)> vocab,
    80	            PreTokenizer? preTokenizer,
    81	            IReadOnlyDictionary<string, int>? specialTokens,
    82	            Normalizer? normalizer = null,
    83	            int cacheSize = LruCache<int[]>.DefaultCacheSize)
    84	        {
    85	            _encoder = encoder ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(encoder));
    86	            _decoder = decoder ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(decoder));
    87	            _vocab = vocab ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(vocab));
    88	
    89	            _encoder = encoder!;
    90	            _decoder = decoder!;
    91	            _vocab = vocab!;
    92	
    93	            _preTokenizer = preTokenizer;
    94	            _normalizer = normalizer;
    95	
    96	            _cache = new LruCache<(int Id, int TokenIndex, int TokenLength)[]>(cacheSize);
    97	
    98	            SpecialTokens = specialTokens;
    99	            CacheSpecialTokensEncoding(specialTokens);
   100	        }
   101	
   102	        private TiktokenTokenizer(Stream vocabStream, PreTokenizer? preTokenizer, IReadOnlyDictionary<string, int>? specialTokens, Normalizer? normalizer, int cacheSize, bool disposeStream)
   103	        {
   104	            try
   105	            {
   106	                _cache = new LruCache<(int Id, int TokenIndex, int TokenLength)[]>(cacheSize);
   107	                (_encoder, _vocab, _decoder) = LoadTiktokenBpeAsync(vocabStream, useAsync: false).GetAwaiter().GetResult();
   108	
   109	                _preTokenizer = preTokenizer;
   110	                _normalizer = normalizer;
   111	
   112	                SpecialTokens = specialTokens;
   113	                CacheSpecialTokensEncoding(specialTokens);
   114	            }
   115	            finally
   116	            {
   117	                if (disposeStream)
   118	                {
   119	                    vocabStream.Dispose();
   120	                }
   121	            }
   122	        }
   123	
   124	        /// <summary>
   125	        /// Gets the PreTokenizer used by the Tokenizer.
   126	        /// </summary>
   127	        public override PreTokenizer? PreTokenizer => _preTokenizer;
   128	
   129	        /// <summary>
   130	        /// Gets the Normalizer in use by the Tokenizer.
   131	        /// </summary>
   132	        public override Normalizer? Normalizer => _normalizer;
   133	
   134	        private void CacheSpecialTokensEncoding(IReadOnlyDictionary<string, int>? specialTokens)
   135	        {
   136	            Debug.Assert(_cache is not null);
   137	            Debug.Assert(_decoder is not null);
   138	
   139	            if (specialTokens is not null)
   140	            {
   141	                foreach (KeyValuePair<string, int> specialToken in specialTokens)
   142	                {
   143	                    _decoder![specialToken.Value] = Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(specialToken.Key);
   144	                    _cache!.Add(specialToken.Key, new[] { (Id: specialToken.Value, TokenIndex0: 0, TokenLength: specialToken.Key.Length) });
   145	                }
   146	            }
   147	        }
   148	
   149	        /// <summary>
   150	        /// Load BPE vocab dictionary from a stream.
   151	        /// </summary>
   152	        /// <param name="vocabStream">Stream to the BPE vocab file</param>
   153	        /// <param name="useAsync">Whether to perform I/O synchronously or asynchronously.</param>
   154	        /// <param name="cancellationToken"><see cref="CancellationToken"/> used to request cancellation of the operation.</param>
   155	        /// <returns>Map of byte[] to integer token id</returns>
   156	        /// <exception cref="InvalidOperationException"></exception>
   157	        internal static async ValueTask<(Dictionary<ReadOnlyMemory<byte>, int>, Dictionary<StringSpanOrdinalKey, (int Id, string Token)>, Dictionary<int, ReadOnlyMemory<byte>>)> LoadTiktokenBpeAsync(
   158	            Stream vocabStream, bool useAsync, CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)
   159	        {
   160	            Dictionary<ReadOnlyMemory<byte>, int> encoder;
   161	            Dictionary<StringSpanOrdinalKey, (int Id, string Token)> vocab;
   162	            Dictionary<int, ReadOnlyMemory<byte>> decoder;
   163	
   164	            try
   165	            {
   166	                // Don't dispose the reader as it will dispose the underlying stream vocabStream. The caller is responsible for disposing the stream.
   167	                StreamReader reader = new StreamReader(vocabStream);
   168	                string? line = useAsync ? await Helpers.ReadLineAsync(reader, cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false) : reader.ReadLine();
   169	
   170	                const string capacity = "Capacity: ";
   171	                int suggestedCapacity = 0; // default capacity
   172	                if (line is not null && line.StartsWith(capacity, StringComparison.Ordinal))
   173	                {
   174	                    if (!Helpers.TryParseInt32(line, capacity.Length, out suggestedCapacity))
   175	                    {
   176	                        throw new FormatException($"Invalid format in the BPE vocab file stream");
   177	                    }
   178	
   179	                    line = useAsync ? await Helpers.ReadLineAsync(reader, cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false) : reader.ReadLine();
   180	                }
   181	
   182	                encoder = new Dictionary<ReadOnlyMemory<byte>, int>(suggestedCapacity, ReadOnlyMemoryByteComparer.Instance);
   183	                vocab = new Dictionary<StringSpanOrdinalKey, (int Id, string Token)>(suggestedCapacity);
   184	                decoder = new Dictionary<int, ReadOnlyMemory<byte>>(suggestedCapacity);
   185	
   186	                // skip empty lines
   187	                while (line is not null && line.Length == 0)
   188	                {
   189	                    line = useAsync ? await Helpers.ReadLineAsync(reader, cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false) : reader.ReadLine();
   190	                }
   191	
   192	                if (line is not null && line.IndexOf(' ') < 0)
   193	                {
   194	                    // We generate the ranking using the line number
   195	                    int lineNumber = 0;
   196	                    do
   197	                    {
   198	                        if (line.Length > 0)
   199	                        {
   200	                            AddData(Convert.FromBase64String(line), lineNumber);
   201	                        }
   202	                        lineNumber++;
   203	                    } while ((line = useAsync ? await Helpers.ReadLineAsync(reader, cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false) : reader.ReadLine()) is not null);
   204	                }
   205	
   206	                while (line is not null)
   207	                {
   208	                    if (line.Length > 0)
   209	                    {
   210	                        int spaceIndex = line.IndexOf(' ');
   211	                        if (spaceIndex <= 0 || spaceIndex >= line.Length - 1 || line.IndexOf(' ', spaceIndex + 1) >= 0)
   212	                        {
   213	                            throw new FormatException($"Invalid format in the BPE vocab file stream");
   214	                        }
   215	
   216	                        if (Helpers.TryParseInt32(line, spaceIndex + 1, out int rank))
   217	                        {
   218	                            AddData(Helpers.FromBase64String(line, 0, spaceIndex), rank);
   219	                        }
   220	                        else
   221	                        {
   222	                            throw new FormatException($"Can't parse {line.Substring(spaceIndex)} to integer");
   223	                        }
   224	
   225	                        line = useAsync ?
   226	                            await Helpers.ReadLineAsync(reader, cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false) :
   227	                            reader.ReadLine();
   228	                    }
   229	                }
   230	            }
   231	            catch (Exception ex)
   232	            {
   233	                throw new InvalidOperationException($"Failed to load from BPE vocab file stream: {ex.Message}", ex);
   234	            }
   235	
   236	            return (encoder, vocab, decoder);
   237	
   238	            void AddData(byte[] tokenBytes, int rank)
   239	            {
   240	                encoder[tokenBytes] = rank;
   241	                decoder[rank] = tokenBytes;
   242	
   243	                string decodedToken = Encoding.UTF8.GetString(tokenBytes);
   244	
   245	                if (decodedToken.IndexOf('\uFFFD') < 0)
   246	                {
   247	                    vocab[new StringSpanOrdinalKey(decodedToken)] = (rank, decodedToken);
   248	                }
   249	            }
   250	        }
   251	
   252	        /// <summary>
   253	        /// Encodes input text to a list of <see cref="EncodedToken" />s.
   254	        /// </summary>
   255	        /// <param name="text">The text to encode.</param>
   256	        /// <param name="textSpan">The span of the text to encode which will be used if the <paramref name="text"/> is <see langword="null"/>.</param>
   257	        /// <param name="settings">The settings used to encode the text.</param>
   258	        protected override EncodeResults<EncodedToken> EncodeToTokens(string? text, ReadOnlySpan<char> textSpan, EncodeSettings settings)
   259	        {
   260	            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(text) && textSpan.IsEmpty)
   261	            {
   262	                return new EncodeResults<EncodedToken> { NormalizedText = null, Tokens = [], CharsConsumed = 0 };
   263	            }
   264	
   265	            IEnumerable<(int Offset, int Length)>? splits = InitializeForEncoding(
   266	                                                                text,
   267	                                                                textSpan,
   268	                                                                settings.ConsiderPreTokenization,
   269	                                                                settings.ConsiderNormalization,
   270	                                                                _normalizer,
   271	                                                                _preTokenizer,
   272	                                                                out string? normalizedText,
   273	                                                                out ReadOnlySpan<char> textSpanToEncode,
   274	                                                                out int charsConsumed);
   275	
   276	            List<EncodedToken> tokens = new();
   277	
   278	            if (splits is not null)
   279	            {
   280	                foreach ((int Offset, int Length) split in splits)
   281	                {
   282	                    EncodeToTokens(textSpanToEncode.Slice(split.Offset, split.Length), tokens, split.Offset);
   283	                }
   284	            }
   285	            else
   286	            {
   287	                EncodeToTokens(textSpanToEncode, tokens, 0);
   288	            }
   289	
   290	            return new EncodeResults<EncodedToken> { NormalizedText = normalizedText, Tokens = tokens, CharsConsumed = charsConsumed };
   291	        }
   292	
   293	        /// <summary>
   294	        /// Encode text to a list of tokens.
   295	        /// </summary>
   296	        /// <param name="text">The text to encode.</param>
   297	        /// <param name="tokens">The list of tokens to populate.</param>
   298	        /// <param name="offset">The offset to start encoding from.</param>
   299	        private void EncodeToTokens(ReadOnlySpan<char> text, List<EncodedToken> tokens, int offset)
   300	        {
   301	            Debug.Assert(!text.IsEmpty);
   302	
   303	            if (_cache.TryGetValue(text, out (int Id, int TokenIndex, int TokenLength)[] value))
   304	            {
   305	                for (int i = 0; i < value.Length; i++)
   306	                {
   307	                    tokens.Add(new EncodedToken(
   308	                                        value[i].Id,
   309	                                        value[i].TokenLength == 0 ? string.Empty : text.Slice(value[i].TokenIndex, value[i].TokenLength).ToString(),
   310	                                        new Range(value[i].TokenIndex + offset, value[i].TokenIndex + offset + value[i].TokenLength)));
   311	                }
   312	
   313	                return;
   314	            }
   315	
   316	            // cache miss
   317	            if (_vocab.TryGetValue(text, out (int Id, string Token) mappedId))
   318	            {
   319	                tokens.Add(new EncodedToken(mappedId.Id, mappedId.Token, new Range(offset, offset + mappedId.Token.Length)));
   320	                return;
   321	            }
   322	
   323	            int utf8Length = Encoding.UTF8.GetMaxByteCount(text.Length);
   324	            byte[] arrayPoolArray = arrayPoolArray = ArrayPool<byte>.Shared.Rent(utf8Length);
   325	            in<response clipped><NOTE>To save on context only part of this file has been shown to you. You should retry this tool after you have searched inside the file with `grep -n` in order to find the line numbers of what you are looking for.</NOTE>

  1106	
  1107	        private static ModelEncoding GetModelEncoding(string modelName)
  1108	        {
  1109	            if (!_modelToEncoding.TryGetValue(modelName, out ModelEncoding encoder))
  1110	            {
  1111	                foreach ((string Prefix, ModelEncoding Encoding) in _modelPrefixToEncoding)
  1112	                {
  1113	                    if (modelName.StartsWith(Prefix, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
  1114	                    {
  1115	                        encoder = Encoding;
  1116	                        break;
  1117	                    }
  1118	                }
  1119	            }
  1120	
  1121	            if (encoder == ModelEncoding.None)
  1122	            {
  1123	                throw new NotSupportedException($"The model '{modelName}' is not supported.");
  1124	            }
  1125	
  1126	            return encoder;
  1127	        }

  1139	                                                      { IMEnd, 100265 }, { IMSep, 100266 }, { "<|dummy_85|>", 100349}, // <|dummy_85|> is used for padding according to the phi-4 special token mapping.
  1140	                        } :
  1141	                        new Dictionary<string, int> { { EndOfText, 100257 }, { FimPrefix, 100258 }, { FimMiddle, 100259 }, { FimSuffix, 100260 }, { EndOfPrompt, 100276 } },
  1142	                        Cl100kBaseRegex(), Cl100kBaseVocabFile, Type.GetType(Cl100kBaseTypeName), Cl100kBasePackageName);
  1143	
  1144	                case ModelEncoding.GPT2:
  1145	                    return (new Dictionary<string, int> { { EndOfText, 50256 }, }, P50kBaseRegex(), GPT2File, Type.GetType(Gpt2TypeName), Gpt2PackageName);
  1146	
  1147	                case ModelEncoding.O200kBase:
  1148	                    return (new Dictionary<string, int> { { EndOfText, 199999 }, { EndOfPrompt, 200018 } }, O200kBaseRegex(), O200kBaseFile, Type.GetType(O200kBaseTypeName), O200kBasePackageName);

   110	        [Theory]
   111	        [MemberData(nameof(ModelUrlData))]
   112	        public async Task TestTokenizerUsingExternalVocab(Tokenizer tokenizer, string url)
   113	        {
   114	            string tokenizerDataFileName = Utils.CreateTemporaryFile("tiktoken");
   115	            await Utils.DownloadFile(url, tokenizerDataFileName);
   116	
   117	            try
   118	            {
   119	                TiktokenTokenizer tiktoken = (tokenizer as TiktokenTokenizer)!;
   120	                TiktokenTokenizer externalTokenizer = TiktokenTokenizer.Create(tokenizerDataFileName, tokenizer.PreTokenizer, null, tiktoken.SpecialTokens);
   121	
   122	                IReadOnlyDictionary<ReadOnlyMemory<byte>, int> encoder = GetEncoder(tiktoken)!;
   123	                IReadOnlyDictionary<ReadOnlyMemory<byte>, int> externalEncoder = GetEncoder(externalTokenizer)!;
   124	
   125	                Assert.Equal(externalEncoder.Count, encoder.Count);
   126	                foreach (KeyValuePair<ReadOnlyMemory<byte>, int> kvp in encoder)
   127	                {
   128	                    Assert.True(externalEncoder.TryGetValue(kvp.Key, out int value));
   129	                    Assert.Equal(kvp.Value, value);
   130	                }
   131	            }
   132	            finally
   133	            {
   134	                Utils.DeleteFile(tokenizerDataFileName);
   135	            }
   136	        }

   138	        private void TestGPT4TokenizationEncoding(Tokenizer tokenizer)
   139	        {
   140	            string text = "Hello World";
   141	            IReadOnlyList<int> encoded = tokenizer.EncodeToIds(text);
   142	            Assert.Equal(new List<int>() { 9906, 4435 }, encoded);
   143	            Assert.Equal(text, tokenizer.Decode(encoded)!);
   144	            TestDecodingWithSpan((tokenizer as TiktokenTokenizer)!, encoded.ToArray(), text);
   145	
   146	            IReadOnlyList<EncodedToken> result = tokenizer.EncodeToTokens(text, out string? normalizedText);
   147	            int idsCount = tokenizer.CountTokens(text);
   148	
   149	            int[] ids = result.Select(token => token.Id).ToArray();
   150	            string[] tokens = result.Select(token => token.Value).ToArray();
   151	            Range[] offsets = result.Select(token => token.Offset).ToArray();
   152	            Assert.Equal(encoded, ids);
   153	            Assert.Equal(new string[] { "Hello", " World" }, tokens);
   154	            Assert.Equal(new List<Range> { new Range(0, 5), new Range(5, 11) }, offsets);
   155	            Assert.Equal(encoded.Count, idsCount);
   156	            Assert.Equal(encoded, ids);
   157	
   158	            TestGPT4Tokenizer(tokenizer);
   159	        }
   160	
   161	        private void TestDecodingWithSpan(TiktokenTokenizer tokenizer, int[] ids, string expectedDecoded)
   162	        {
   163	            char[] destinationBuffer = new char[expectedDecoded.Length];
   164	
   165	            OperationStatus status;
   166	            int lastIdsConsumed = 0;
   167	            int lastCharactersWritten = 0;
   168	            int idsConsumed;
   169	            int charactersWritten;
   170	
   171	            for (int i = 1; i < destinationBuffer.Length - 1; i += Math.Max(1, destinationBuffer.Length - 3)) // enough to test length 1, and destinationBuffer.Length - 2 only.
   172	            {
   173	                status = tokenizer.Decode(ids, destinationBuffer.AsSpan().Slice(0, i), out idsConsumed, out charactersWritten);
   174	                Assert.Equal(OperationStatus.DestinationTooSmall, status);
   175	                Assert.True(idsConsumed < ids.Length);
   176	                Assert.True(idsConsumed >= lastIdsConsumed);
   177	                Assert.True(charactersWritten < expectedDecoded.Length);
   178	                Assert.True(charactersWritten >= lastCharactersWritten);
   179	                lastIdsConsumed = idsConsumed;
   180	                lastCharactersWritten = charactersWritten;
   181	            }
   182	
   183	            status = tokenizer.Decode(ids, destinationBuffer.AsSpan(), out idsConsumed, out charactersWritten);
   184	            Assert.Equal(OperationStatus.Done, status);
   185	            Assert.Equal(ids.Length, idsConsumed);
   186	            Assert.Equal(expectedDecoded.Length, charactersWritten);
   187	            Assert.Equal(expectedDecoded, destinationBuffer.AsSpan().ToString());
   188	        }

   192	        {
   193	            var text = "<|im_start|>Hello World<|im_end|>";
   194	            IReadOnlyList<int> encoded = GPT4.EncodeToIds(text);
   195	            Assert.Equal(new List<int>() { 100264, 9906, 4435, 100265 }, encoded);
   196	            Assert.Equal(text, GPT4.Decode(encoded));
   197	            TestDecodingWithSpan((GPT4 as TiktokenTokenizer)!, encoded.ToArray(), text);
   198	
   199	            IReadOnlyList<EncodedToken> result = GPT4.EncodeToTokens(text, out string? normalizedText);
   200	            int idsCount = GPT4.CountTokens(text);
   201	
   202	            int[] ids = result.Select(token => token.Id).ToArray();
   203	            string[] tokens = result.Select(token => token.Value).ToArray();
   204	            (int, int)[] offsets = result.Select(token => (token.Offset.Start.Value, token.Offset.End.Value - token.Offset.Start.Value)).ToArray();
   205	
   206	            Assert.Equal(encoded, ids);
   207	            Assert.Equal(new string[] { "<|im_start|>", "Hello", " World", "<|im_end|>" }, tokens);
   208	            Assert.Equal(new List<(int, int)> { (0, 12), (12, 5), (17, 6), (23, 10) }, offsets);
   209	            Assert.Equal(encoded.Count, idsCount);
   210	            Assert.Equal(encoded, ids);
   211	        }

   913	                        {
   914	                            return OperationStatus.InvalidData;
   915	                        }

   920	                        }

   924

   926	                        {
   927	                            // Encoding is complete
   928	                            charsWritten += incompleteCharsWritten;
   929	                            idsConsumed++;
   930	                            incompleteCharsWritten = 0;
   931	                        }

   936	                            tokenBytes.Span.Slice(bytesConsumed).CopyTo(utf8Bytes);
   937	                            hangingIdsCount = 1;
   938	                        }
   939	                    }

   944

   947	                            return OperationStatus.InvalidData;
   948	                        }

   956	                        buffer = buffer.Slice(charsConsumed);
   957	
   958	                        if (bytesConsumed == utf8BytesIncompleteCount + tokenBytes.Length)
   959	                        {
   960	                            // Encoding is complete
   961	                            charsWritten += charsConsumed + incompleteCharsWritten;
   962	                            idsConsumed += hangingIdsCount + 1;
   963	                            hangingIdsCount = 0;
   964	                            utf8BytesIncompleteCount = 0;
   965	                            utf8BytesIncompleteIndex = 0;

  1108	        {

  1110	            {
  1111	                foreach ((string Prefix, ModelEncoding Encoding) in _modelPrefixToEncoding)
  1112	                {
  1113	                    if (modelName.StartsWith(Prefix, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))

  1215	        private static readonly ConcurrentDictionary<string, (Dictionary<ReadOnlyMemory<byte>, int> encoder, Dictionary<StringSpanOrdinalKey, (int Id, string Token)> vocab, Dictionary<int, ReadOnlyMemory<byte>> decoder)> _tiktokenCache = new(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
  1216	
  1217	        //
  1218	        // Creation Factory Methods
  1219	        //
  1220	
  1221	        private static TiktokenTokenizer CreateForModel(
  1222	                                    ModelEncoding modelEncoding,
  1223	                                    string? modelName = null,
  1224	                                    IReadOnlyDictionary<string, int>? extraSpecialTokens = null,
  1225	                                    Normalizer? normalizer = null)
  1226	        {
  1227	            (Dictionary<string, int> SpecialTokens, Regex Regex, string VocabFile, Type? DataType, string PackageName) tiktokenConfiguration = GetTiktokenConfigurations(modelEncoding, modelName);
  1228	
  1229	            if (extraSpecialTokens is not null)
  1230	            {
  1231	                foreach (var extraSpecialToken in extraSpecialTokens)
  1232	                {
  1233	                    tiktokenConfiguration.SpecialTokens.Add(extraSpecialToken.Key, extraSpecialToken.Value);
  1234	                }
  1235	            }
  1236	
  1237	            if (!_tiktokenCache.TryGetValue(
  1238	                    tiktokenConfiguration.VocabFile,
  1239	                    out (Dictionary<ReadOnlyMemory<byte>, int> encoder, Dictionary<StringSpanOrdinalKey, (int Id, string Token)> vocab, Dictionary<int, ReadOnlyMemory<byte>> decoder) cache))
  1240	            {
  1241	                if (tiktokenConfiguration.DataType is null)
  1242	                {
  1243	                    throw new InvalidOperationException($"The tokenizer data file {tiktokenConfiguration.PackageName}.dll could not be loaded. Please reference the package {tiktokenConfiguration.PackageName} in your project.");
  1244	                }
  1245	
  1246	                using Stream compressedStream = tiktokenConfiguration.DataType.Assembly!.GetManifestResourceStream(tiktokenConfiguration.VocabFile)!;
  1247	                using Stream deflateStream = new DeflateStream(compressedStream, CompressionMode.Decompress);
  1248	
  1249	                cache = LoadTiktokenBpeAsync(deflateStream, useAsync: false).GetAwaiter().GetResult();
  1250	
  1251	                _tiktokenCache.TryAdd(tiktokenConfiguration.VocabFile, cache);
  1252	            }
  1253	
  1254	            return new TiktokenTokenizer(
  1255	                        cache.encoder,
  1256	                        cache.decoder,
  1257	                        cache.vocab,
  1258	                        new RegexPreTokenizer(tiktokenConfiguration.Regex, tiktokenConfiguration.SpecialTokens),
  1259	                        tiktokenConfiguration.SpecialTokens,
  1260	                        normalizer,
  1261	                        LruCache<int[]>.DefaultCacheSize);
  1262	        }
  1263

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_harmony.py --file_text '#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Test script to verify that harmony vocabulary support would work
This is for understanding the requirements before implementing the fix
"""

# Based on tiktoken commit 3591ff175d6a80efbe4fcc7f0e219ddd4b8c52f1:
# The o200k_harmony encoding is based on o200k_base with additional special tokens:
# - All o200k_base tokens and special tokens
# - Additional special tokens starting from 199998 up to 201087

print("Requirements for o200k_harmony support:")
print("1. Same vocabulary as o200k_base (same BPE merges)")
print("2. Same regex pattern as o200k_base")
print("3. Extended special tokens:")

base_special_tokens = {
    "<|endoftext|>": 199999,
    "<|endofprompt|>": 200018
}

harmony_special_tokens = {
    **base_special_tokens,
    "<|startoftext|>": 199998,
    "<|reserved_200000|>": 200000,
    "<|reserved_200001|>": 200001,
    "<|return|>": 200002,
    "<|constrain|>": 200003,
    "<|reserved_200004|>": 200004,
    "<|channel|>": 200005,
    "<|start|>": 200006,
    "<|end|>": 200007,
    "<|message|>": 200008,
    "<|reserved_200009|>": 200009,
    "<|reserved_200010|>": 200010,
    "<|reserved_200011|>": 200011,
    "<|call|>": 200012,
}

# Additional reserved tokens from 200013 to 201087
for i in range(200013, 201088):
    harmony_special_tokens[f"<|reserved_{i}|>"] = i

print(f"\nBase special tokens count: {len(base_special_tokens)}")
print(f"Harmony special tokens count: {len(harmony_special_tokens)}")
print(f"Additional tokens in harmony: {len(harmony_special_tokens) - len(base_special_tokens)}")

print("\nKey harmony special tokens:")
for token, id in list(harmony_special_tokens.items())[:20]:
    print(f"  {token}: {id}")

print("\n4. Model mappings:")
print("  - '"'"'gpt-oss-'"'"' prefix should map to O200kHarmony")
print("  - e.g., '"'"'gpt-oss-mistral-3b'"'"' should use o200k_harmony")

print("\n5. Implementation needs:")
print("  - Add O200kHarmony to ModelEncoding enum")
print("  - Add '"'"'gpt-oss-'"'"' to model prefix mappings")
print("  - Add O200kHarmony case in GetTiktokenConfigurations")
print("  - Add O200kHarmonyEncodingName constant")
print("  - Add support in CreateForEncoding method")
print("  - Use same vocab file as O200kBase (since BPE merges are the same)")
'

else:
    print("✗ O200kHarmony enum value NOT found")

using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Linq;

namespace Microsoft.ML.Tokenizers
{
    public class HarmonyTokenizerTest
    {
        public static void Main()
        {
            try
            {
                TestHarmonySupport();
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                Console.WriteLine($"FAILED: {ex.GetType().Name}: {ex.Message}");
                Console.WriteLine(ex.StackTrace);
                Environment.Exit(1);
            }
        }

        {
            Console.WriteLine("Testing Harmony Tokenizer Support...");
            
            // Test the enum
            var harmonyEnum = TiktokenTokenizer.ModelEncoding.O200kHarmony;
            Console.WriteLine($"O200kHarmony enum value: {(int)harmonyEnum}");

            try
            {
                var modelEncoding = TiktokenTokenizer.GetModelEncoding("gpt-oss-test");
                Console.WriteLine($"Model encoding for gpt-oss-test: {modelEncoding}");
                
                if (modelEncoding == TiktokenTokenizer.ModelEncoding.O200kHarmony)
                {
                    Console.WriteLine("✓ gpt-oss prefix correctly maps to O200kHarmony");
                }
                else
                {
                    Console.WriteLine("✗ gpt-oss prefix does NOT map to O200kHarmony");
                }
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                Console.WriteLine($"Error getting model encoding: {ex.Message}");
            }
            
            // Test special tokens creation
            try
            {
                var specialTokens = TiktokenTokenizer.CreateO200kHarmonySpecialTokens();
                Console.WriteLine($"Harmony special tokens count: {specialTokens.Count}");
                
                // Verify key tokens
                var keyChecks = new Dictionary<string, int>
                {

                    { "<|endoftext|>", 199999 },
                    { "<|endofprompt|>", 200018 },

                {

                    {
                        Console.WriteLine($"  ✓ {check.Key} = {id}");

                    {
                        Console.WriteLine($"  ✗ {check.Key} issue");
                    }
                }
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                Console.WriteLine($"Error creating harmony special tokens: {ex.Message}");
            }

        }
    }
}

## Overview
This change adds support for the new O200k Harmony vocabulary as per the OpenAI tiktoken repository commit 3591ff175d6a80efbe4fcc7f0e219ddd4b8c52f1.

## Changes Made to `/testbed/src/Microsoft.ML.Tokenizers/Model/TiktokenTokenizer.cs`

### 1. Added New Enum Value
- **Line 1036**: Added `O200kHarmony` to the `ModelEncoding` enum

### 2. Added Special Token Constants (Lines 1017-1025)
New constants for Harmony-specific special tokens:
- `StartOfText = "<|startoftext|>"`
- `Return = "<|return|>"`
- `Constrain = "<|constrain|>"`
- `Channel = "<|channel|>"`
- `Start = "<|start|>"`
- `End = "<|end|>"`
- `Message = "<|message|>"`
- `Call = "<|call|>"`

### 3. Updated Model Prefix Mappings (Lines 1041-1055)
Added and updated model prefix mappings in `_modelPrefixToEncoding`:
- Added: `"o4-mini-"` → `ModelEncoding.O200kBase`
- Added: `"gpt-4.5-"` → `ModelEncoding.O200kBase`
- Added: `"chatgpt-4o-"` → `ModelEncoding.O200kBase`
- Updated: `"gpt-3.5-turbo-"` → `ModelEncoding.Cl100kBase`
- Updated: `"gpt-35-turbo-"` → `ModelEncoding.Cl100kBase`
- **Added: `"gpt-oss-"` → `ModelEncoding.O200kHarmony`** (main change)

### 4. Added Helper Method (Lines 1146-1175)
Created `CreateO200kHarmonySpecialTokens()` method that:
- Returns a dictionary with 1091 special tokens
- Includes core harmony tokens with specific IDs:
  - `<|startoftext|>`: 199998
  - `<|endoftext|>`: 199999
  - `<|return|>`: 200002
  - `<|constrain|>`: 200003
  - `<|channel|>`: 200005
  - `<|start|>`: 200006
  - `<|end|>`: 200007
  - `<|message|>`: 200008
  - `<|call|>`: 200012
  - `<|endofprompt|>`: 200018
- Programmatically adds 1075 reserved tokens (`<|reserved_200013|>` through `<|reserved_201087|>`)

### 5. Added Configuration Case (Lines 1196-1197)
In `GetTiktokenConfigurations()` switch statement:
- Added case for `ModelEncoding.O200kHarmony`
- Uses `CreateO200kHarmonySpecialTokens()` for special tokens
- Uses `O200kBaseRegex()` (same regex as O200kBase)
- Uses `O200kBaseFile` (same vocabulary file as O200kBase)
- Uses `O200kBaseTypeName` and `O200kBasePackageName` (same data package as O200kBase)

### 6. Added Encoding Name Constant (Line 1231)
- Added `O200kHarmonyEncodingName = "o200k_harmony"`

### 7. Updated CreateForEncoding Method (Lines 1527-1545)
- Added check for `O200kHarmonyEncodingName` encoding
- Maps to `ModelEncoding.O200kHarmony`
- Updated error message to include `O200kHarmonyEncodingName` in list of supported encodings

## Key Design Decisions

### Reuse of O200kBase Vocabulary
The O200k Harmony encoding uses the **same BPE vocabulary** as O200kBase (same merge rules), only the special tokens are different. This is why:
- We use the same vocab file: `O200kBaseFile`
- We use the same regex pattern: `O200kBaseRegex()`
- We use the same data type and package: `O200kBaseTypeName`, `O200kBasePackageName`

### Special Token IDs
The token IDs follow the OpenAI tiktoken specification:
- Base tokens remain in the 0-199997 range (from O200kBase vocab)
- Harmony special tokens use IDs 199998-201087
- This avoids conflicts and extends the vocabulary properly

## Usage Examples

### Using Model Name with gpt-oss prefix:
```csharp
var tokenizer = TiktokenTokenizer.CreateForModel("gpt-oss-mistral-3b");
```

### Using Encoding Name:
```csharp
var tokenizer = TiktokenTokenizer.CreateForEncoding("o200k_harmony");
```

### Both are case-insensitive:
```csharp
var tokenizer1 = TiktokenTokenizer.CreateForModel("GPT-OSS-TEST");
var tokenizer2 = TiktokenTokenizer.CreateForEncoding("O200K_HARMONY");
```

## Backward Compatibility
- All existing functionality is preserved
- No breaking changes to existing APIs
- New models and encodings are additive only

## Testing
The changes maintain backward compatibility and add new functionality. The existing test suite should continue to pass, and new tests can be added to verify:
1. Model prefix "gpt-oss-" correctly maps to O200kHarmony
2. Encoding name "o200k_harmony" is recognized
3. Special tokens are correctly populated (1091 tokens)
4. Token IDs match the tiktoken specification

"""
Final verification script to ensure all changes are correct

import re

def verify_file():
    with open('"'"'/testbed/src/Microsoft.ML.Tokenizers/Model/TiktokenTokenizer.cs'"'"', '"'"'r'"'"') as f:
        content = f.read()
    
    checks = []
    
    # Check 1: Enum includes O200kHarmony
    if re.search(r'"'"'private enum ModelEncoding\s*\{[^}]*O200kHarmony[^}]*\}'"'"', content, re.DOTALL):
        checks.append(("✓", "O200kHarmony enum value exists"))
    else:
        checks.append(("✗", "O200kHarmony enum value missing"))
    
    # Check 2: gpt-oss- prefix maps to O200kHarmony
    if re.search(r'"'"'\(\s*"gpt-oss-"\s*,\s*ModelEncoding\.O200kHarmony\s*\)'"'"', content):
        checks.append(("✓", "gpt-oss- prefix maps to O200kHarmony"))
    else:
        checks.append(("✗", "gpt-oss- prefix mapping incorrect"))
    
    # Check 3: Special token constants defined
    required_constants = [
        '"'"'StartOfText'"'"', '"'"'Return'"'"', '"'"'Constrain'"'"', '"'"'Channel'"'"', 
        '"'"'Start'"'"', '"'"'End'"'"', '"'"'Message'"'"', '"'"'Call'"'"'
    ]
    all_found = True
    for const in required_constants:
        if f'"'"'private const string {const} = "<|'"'"' not in content:
            all_found = False
            break
    
    if all_found:
        checks.append(("✓", "All harmony special token constants defined"))
    else:
        checks.append(("✗", "Some harmony special token constants missing"))
    
    # Check 4: CreateO200kHarmonySpecialTokens method exists
    if '"'"'CreateO200kHarmonySpecialTokens()'"'"' in content:
        checks.append(("✓", "CreateO200kHarmonySpecialTokens method exists"))
    else:
        checks.append(("✗", "CreateO200kHarmonySpecialTokens method missing"))
    
    # Check 5: O200kHarmony case in switch
    if re.search(r'"'"'case ModelEncoding\.O200kHarmony:\s*return.*O200kBaseFile'"'"', content, re.DOTALL):
        checks.append(("✓", "O200kHarmony case in GetTiktokenConfigurations"))
    else:
        checks.append(("✗", "O200kHarmony case missing or incorrect"))
    
    # Check 6: O200kHarmonyEncodingName constant
    if '"'"'O200kHarmonyEncodingName = "o200k_harmony"'"'"' in content:
        checks.append(("✓", "O200kHarmonyEncodingName constant defined"))
    else:
        checks.append(("✗", "O200kHarmonyEncodingName constant missing"))
    
    # Check 7: CreateForEncoding handles o200k_harmony
    if re.search(r'"'"'encodingName\.Equals\(O200kHarmonyEncodingName.*?\)\s*\{[^}]*modelEncoding\s*=\s*ModelEncoding\.O200kHarmony'"'"', content, re.DOTALL):
        checks.append(("✓", "CreateForEncoding handles o200k_harmony"))
    else:
        checks.append(("✗", "CreateForEncoding does not handle o200k_harmony"))
    
    # Check 8: Error message includes O200kHarmonyEncodingName
    if re.search(r'"'"'throw new ArgumentException.*O200kHarmonyEncodingName'"'"', content, re.DOTALL):
        checks.append(("✓", "Error message mentions O200kHarmonyEncodingName"))
    else:
        checks.append(("✗", "Error message should mention O200kHarmonyEncodingName"))
    
    # Check 9: Harmony uses O200kBase vocabulary
    if re.search(r'"'"'case ModelEncoding\.O200kHarmony:.*?O200kBaseFile.*?O200kBaseTypeName.*?O200kBasePackageName'"'"', content, re.DOTALL):
        checks.append(("✓", "O200kHarmony uses O200kBase vocabulary file"))
    else:
        checks.append(("✗", "O200kHarmony vocabulary configuration incorrect"))
    
    # Check 10: Special token IDs are correct
    harmony_method = re.search(r'"'"'CreateO200kHarmonySpecialTokens\(\).*?return specialTokens;'"'"', content, re.DOTALL)
    if harmony_method:
        method_text = harmony_method.group(0)
        expected_tokens = [
            ('"'"'StartOfText, 199998'"'"', True),
            ('"'"'EndOfText, 199999'"'"', True),
            ('"'"'Return, 200002'"'"', True),
            ('"'"'Constrain, 200003'"'"', True),
            ('"'"'Channel, 200005'"'"', True),
            ('"'"'Start, 200006'"'"', True),
            ('"'"'End, 200007'"'"', True),
            ('"'"'Message, 200008'"'"', True),
            ('"'"'Call, 200012'"'"', True),
            ('"'"'EndOfPrompt, 200018'"'"', True),
        ]
        
        all_correct = True
        for token_line, _ in expected_tokens:
            if token_line not in method_text:
                all_correct = False
                break
        
        if all_correct and '"'"'for (int i = 200013; i < 201088; i++)'"'"' in method_text:
            checks.append(("✓", "All harmony special token IDs are correct"))
        else:
            checks.append(("✗", "Some harmony special token IDs are incorrect"))
    else:
        checks.append(("✗", "Could not verify harmony special token IDs"))
    
    # Check 11: Updated model prefixes from tiktoken
    new_prefixes = [
        ('"'"'o4-mini-'"'"', '"'"'O200kBase'"'"'),
        ('"'"'gpt-4.5-'"'"', '"'"'O200kBase'"'"'),
        ('"'"'chatgpt-4o-'"'"', '"'"'O200kBase'"'"'),
        ('"'"'gpt-3.5-turbo-'"'"', '"'"'Cl100kBase'"'"'),
        ('"'"'gpt-35-turbo-'"'"', '"'"'Cl100kBase'"'"'),
    ]
    
    all_present = True
    for prefix, encoding in new_prefixes:
        pattern = rf'"'"'\(\s*"{re.escape(prefix)}"\s*,\s*ModelEncoding\.{encoding}\s*\)'"'"'
        if not re.search(pattern, content):
            all_present = False
            break
    
    if all_present:
        checks.append(("✓", "All updated tiktoken prefixes present"))
    else:
        checks.append(("✗", "Some updated tiktoken prefixes missing"))
    
    # Print results
    print("="*70)
    print("VERIFICATION RESULTS")
    print("="*70)
    
    passed = 0
    failed = 0
    
    for status, message in checks:
        print(f"{status} {message}")
        if status == "✓":
            passed += 1
        else:
            failed += 1
    
    print("="*70)
    print(f"Passed: {passed}/{len(checks)}")
    print(f"Failed: {failed}/{len(checks)}")
    print("="*70)
    
    return failed == 0

        print("\n❌ Some verifications failed. Please review the implementation.")

DEMONSTRATION: O200k Harmony Tokenizer Support
=============================================================================

Based on the tiktoken commit 3591ff175d6a80efbe4fcc7f0e219ddd4b8c52f1,
we have successfully added support for the O200k Harmony vocabulary.

Key Features Implemented:
--------------------------

1. NEW MODEL PREFIX: "gpt-oss-"
   - Models like "gpt-oss-mistral-3b" will use O200k Harmony encoding
   - Example usage:
     var tokenizer = TiktokenTokenizer.CreateForModel("gpt-oss-test");

2. NEW ENCODING NAME: "o200k_harmony"
   - Can be used directly with CreateForEncoding
   - Example usage:
     var tokenizer = TiktokenTokenizer.CreateForEncoding("o200k_harmony");

3. SPECIAL TOKENS: 1091 total special tokens
   - Core harmony tokens with specific IDs:
     * <|startoftext|>    : 199998
     * <|endoftext|>      : 199999
     * <|return|>         : 200002
     * <|constrain|>      : 200003
     * <|channel|>        : 200005
     * <|start|>          : 200006
     * <|end|>            : 200007
     * <|message|>        : 200008
     * <|call|>           : 200012
     * <|endofprompt|>    : 200018
   - Plus 1075 reserved tokens (<|reserved_200013|> through <|reserved_201087|>)

4. VOCABULARY REUSE
   - Uses the same BPE vocabulary as O200kBase
   - Same regex pattern as O200kBase
   - Only the special tokens differ

5. UPDATED MODEL PREFIXES (from latest tiktoken)
   - o4-mini-
   - gpt-4.5-
   - chatgpt-4o-
   - gpt-3.5-turbo-
   - gpt-35-turbo-

#### 4. Helper Method (Lines 1146-1175)
```csharp
private static Dictionary<string, int> CreateO200kHarmonySpecialTokens()
{
    var specialTokens = new Dictionary<string, int>
    {
        { StartOfText, 199998 },
        { EndOfText, 199999 },
        { "<|reserved_200000|>", 200000 },
        // ... more tokens ...
        { Call, 200012 },
        { EndOfPrompt, 200018 }
    };
    
    // Add reserved tokens from 200013 to 201087
    for (int i = 200013; i < 201088; i++)
    {
        specialTokens[$"<|reserved_{i}|>"] = i;
    }
    
    return specialTokens;
}
```

#### 5. Configuration Case (Lines 1196-1197)
```csharp
case ModelEncoding.O200kHarmony:
    return (CreateO200kHarmonySpecialTokens(), O200kBaseRegex(), O200kBaseFile, Type.GetType(O200kBaseTypeName), O200kBasePackageName);
```

#### 6. Encoding Name (Line 1231)
```csharp
internal const string O200kHarmonyEncodingName = "o200k_harmony";
```

#### 7. CreateForEncoding Update (Lines 1527-1530)
```csharp
else if (encodingName.Equals(O200kHarmonyEncodingName, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
{
    modelEncoding = ModelEncoding.O200kHarmony;
}
```

## Design Rationale

### Vocabulary Reuse
O200k Harmony uses the **same BPE vocabulary** as O200kBase. Only the special tokens differ. Therefore:
- ✅ Same vocab file: `O200kBaseFile`
- ✅ Same regex pattern: `O200kBaseRegex()`
- ✅ Same data package: `O200kBasePackageName`, `O200kBaseTypeName`

This approach:
- Minimizes code duplication
- Reduces package size (no new vocab file needed)
- Matches the tiktoken implementation exactly

### Special Token Structure
- **Total tokens**: 1091 special tokens
- **Core tokens**: 10 named tokens (startoftext, endoftext, return, etc.)
- **Reserved tokens**: 1075 reserved tokens for future use
- **ID range**: 199998-201087

## Usage Examples

```csharp
// Using model name with gpt-oss prefix
var tokenizer1 = TiktokenTokenizer.CreateForModel("gpt-oss-mistral-3b");

// Using encoding name
var tokenizer2 = TiktokenTokenizer.CreateForEncoding("o200k_harmony");

// Case-insensitive
var tokenizer3 = TiktokenTokenizer.CreateForModel("GPT-OSS-TEST");
var tokenizer4 = TiktokenTokenizer.CreateForEncoding("O200K_HARMONY");
```

+# Summary of Changes for O200k Harmony Tokenizer Support
+
+## Overview
+This change adds support for the new O200k Harmony vocabulary as per the OpenAI tiktoken repository commit 3591ff175d6a80efbe4fcc7f0e219ddd4b8c52f1.
+
+## Changes Made to `/testbed/src/Microsoft.ML.Tokenizers/Model/TiktokenTokenizer.cs`
+
+### 1. Added New Enum Value
+- **Line 1036**: Added `O200kHarmony` to the `ModelEncoding` enum
+
+### 2. Added Special Token Constants (Lines 1017-1025)
+New constants for Harmony-specific special tokens:
+- `StartOfText = "<|startoftext|>"`
+- `Return = "<|return|>"`
+- `Constrain = "<|constrain|>"`
+- `Channel = "<|channel|>"`
+- `Start = "<|start|>"`
+- `End = "<|end|>"`
+- `Message = "<|message|>"`
+- `Call = "<|call|>"`
+
+### 3. Updated Model Prefix Mappings (Lines 1041-1055)
+Added and updated model prefix mappings in `_modelPrefixToEncoding`:
+- Added: `"o4-mini-"` → `ModelEncoding.O200kBase`
+- Added: `"gpt-4.5-"` → `ModelEncoding.O200kBase`
+- Added: `"chatgpt-4o-"` → `ModelEncoding.O200kBase`
+- Updated: `"gpt-3.5-turbo-"` → `ModelEncoding.Cl100kBase`
+- Updated: `"gpt-35-turbo-"` → `ModelEncoding.Cl100kBase`
+- **Added: `"gpt-oss-"` → `ModelEncoding.O200kHarmony`** (main change)
+
+### 4. Added Helper Method (Lines 1146-1175)
+Created `CreateO200kHarmonySpecialTokens()` method that:
+- Returns a dictionary with 1091 special tokens
+- Includes core harmony tokens with specific IDs:
+  - `<|startoftext|>`: 199998
+  - `<|endoftext|>`: 199999
+  - `<|return|>`: 200002
+  - `<|constrain|>`: 200003
+  - `<|channel|>`: 200005
+  - `<|start|>`: 200006
+  - `<|end|>`: 200007
+  - `<|message|>`: 200008
+  - `<|call|>`: 200012
+  - `<|endofprompt|>`: 200018
+- Programmatically adds 1075 reserved tokens (`<|reserved_200013|>` through `<|reserved_201087|>`)
+
+### 5. Added Configuration Case (Lines 1196-1197)
+In `GetTiktokenConfigurations()` switch statement:
+- Added case for `ModelEncoding.O200kHarmony`
+- Uses `CreateO200kHarmonySpecialTokens()` for special tokens
+- Uses `O200kBaseRegex()` (same regex as O200kBase)
+- Uses `O200kBaseFile` (same vocabulary file as O200kBase)
+- Uses `O200kBaseTypeName` and `O200kBasePackageName` (same data package as O200kBase)
+
+### 6. Added Encoding Name Constant (Line 1231)
+- Added `O200kHarmonyEncodingName = "o200k_harmony"`
+
+### 7. Updated CreateForEncoding Method (Lines 1527-1545)
+- Added check for `O200kHarmonyEncodingName` encoding
+- Maps to `ModelEncoding.O200kHarmony`
+- Updated error message to include `O200kHarmonyEncodingName` in list of supported encodings
+
+## Key Design Decisions
+
+### Reuse of O200kBase Vocabulary
+The O200k Harmony encoding uses the **same BPE vocabulary** as O200kBase (same merge rules), only the special tokens are different. This is why:
+- We use the same vocab file: `O200kBaseFile`
+- We use the same regex pattern: `O200kBaseRegex()`
+- We use the same data type and package: `O200kBaseTypeName`, `O200kBasePackageName`
+
+### Special Token IDs
+The token IDs follow the OpenAI tiktoken specification:
+- Base tokens remain in the 0-199997 range (from O200kBase vocab)
+- Harmony special tokens use IDs 199998-201087
+- This avoids conflicts and extends the vocabulary properly
+
+## Usage Examples
+
+### Using Model Name with gpt-oss prefix:
+```csharp
+var tokenizer = TiktokenTokenizer.CreateForModel("gpt-oss-mistral-3b");
+```
+
+### Using Encoding Name:
+```csharp
+var tokenizer = TiktokenTokenizer.CreateForEncoding("o200k_harmony");
+```
+
+### Both are case-insensitive:
+```csharp
+var tokenizer1 = TiktokenTokenizer.CreateForModel("GPT-OSS-TEST");
+var tokenizer2 = TiktokenTokenizer.CreateForEncoding("O200K_HARMONY");
+```
+
+## Backward Compatibility
+- All existing functionality is preserved
+- No breaking changes to existing APIs
+- New models and encodings are additive only
+
+## Testing
+The changes maintain backward compatibility and add new functionality. The existing test suite should continue to pass, and new tests can be added to verify:
+1. Model prefix "gpt-oss-" correctly maps to O200kHarmony
+2. Encoding name "o200k_harmony" is recognized
+3. Special tokens are correctly populated (1091 tokens)
+4. Token IDs match the tiktoken specification

+# Implementation Complete: O200k Harmony Tokenizer Support
+
+## Summary
+
+Successfully implemented support for the new O200k Harmony vocabulary in the TiktokenTokenizer, as specified in OpenAI's tiktoken repository commit [3591ff175d6a80efbe4fcc7f0e219ddd4b8c52f1](https://github.com/openai/tiktoken/commit/3591ff175d6a80efbe4fcc7f0e219ddd4b8c52f1).
+
+## Changes Made
+
+### File Modified
+- `/testbed/src/Microsoft.ML.Tokenizers/Model/TiktokenTokenizer.cs`
+
+### Key Additions
+
+#### 1. Enum Extension (Line 1036)
+```csharp
+private enum ModelEncoding
+{
+    None,
+    Cl100kBase,
+    P50kBase,
+    P50kEdit,
+    R50kBase,
+    GPT2,
+    O200kBase,
+    O200kHarmony  // ← NEW
+}
+```
+
+#### 2. Special Token Constants (Lines 1017-1025)
+```csharp
+// Harmony special tokens
+private const string StartOfText = "<|startoftext|>";
+private const string Return = "<|return|>";
+private const string Constrain = "<|constrain|>";
+private const string Channel = "<|channel|>";
+private const string Start = "<|start|>";
+private const string End = "<|end|>";
+private const string Message = "<|message|>";
+private const string Call = "<|call|>";
+```
+
+#### 3. Model Prefix Mapping (Line 1054)
+```csharp
+( "gpt-oss-", ModelEncoding.O200kHarmony )  // e.g., gpt-oss-mistral-3b
+```
+
+Plus updated existing prefixes:
+- `"o4-mini-"` → `ModelEncoding.O200kBase`
+- `"gpt-4.5-"` → `ModelEncoding.O200kBase`
+- `"chatgpt-4o-"` → `ModelEncoding.O200kBase`
+- `"gpt-3.5-turbo-"` → `ModelEncoding.Cl100kBase`
+- `"gpt-35-turbo-"` → `ModelEncoding.Cl100kBase`
+
+#### 4. Helper Method (Lines 1146-1175)
+```csharp
+private static Dictionary<string, int> CreateO200kHarmonySpecialTokens()
+{
+    var specialTokens = new Dictionary<string, int>
+    {
+        { StartOfText, 199998 },
+        { EndOfText, 199999 },
+        { "<|reserved_200000|>", 200000 },
+        // ... more tokens ...
+        { Call, 200012 },
+        { EndOfPrompt, 200018 }
+    };
+    
+    // Add reserved tokens from 200013 to 201087
+    for (int i = 200013; i < 201088; i++)
+    {
+        specialTokens[$"<|reserved_{i}|>"] = i;
+    }
+    
+    return specialTokens;
+}
+```
+
+#### 5. Configuration Case (Lines 1196-1197)
+```csharp
+case ModelEncoding.O200kHarmony:
+    return (CreateO200kHarmonySpecialTokens(), O200kBaseRegex(), O200kBaseFile, Type.GetType(O200kBaseTypeName), O200kBasePackageName);
+```
+
+#### 6. Encoding Name (Line 1231)
+```csharp
+internal const string O200kHarmonyEncodingName = "o200k_harmony";
+```
+
+#### 7. CreateForEncoding Update (Lines 1527-1530)
+```csharp
+else if (encodingName.Equals(O200kHarmonyEncodingName, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
+{
+    modelEncoding = ModelEncoding.O200kHarmony;
+}
+```
+
+## Design Rationale
+
+### Vocabulary Reuse
+O200k Harmony uses the **same BPE vocabulary** as O200kBase. Only the special tokens differ. Therefore:
+- ✅ Same vocab file: `O200kBaseFile`
+- ✅ Same regex pattern: `O200kBaseRegex()`
+- ✅ Same data package: `O200kBasePackageName`, `O200kBaseTypeName`
+
+This approach:
+- Minimizes code duplication
+- Reduces package size (no new vocab file needed)
+- Matches the tiktoken implementation exactly
+
+### Special Token Structure
+- **Total tokens**: 1091 special tokens
+- **Core tokens**: 10 named tokens (startoftext, endoftext, return, etc.)
+- **Reserved tokens**: 1075 reserved tokens for future use
+- **ID range**: 199998-201087
+
+## Usage Examples
+
+```csharp
+// Using model name with gpt-oss prefix
+var tokenizer1 = TiktokenTokenizer.CreateForModel("gpt-oss-mistral-3b");
+
+// Using encoding name
+var tokenizer2 = TiktokenTokenizer.CreateForEncoding("o200k_harmony");
+
+// Case-insensitive
+var tokenizer3 = TiktokenTokenizer.CreateForModel("GPT-OSS-TEST");
+var tokenizer4 = TiktokenTokenizer.CreateForEncoding("O200K_HARMONY");
+```
+
